on ui_control(xy_center_circles{real[]} {xy_center_circles} ){thread-unsafe}
	cc_cb_id{int} {cc_cb_id}  := NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} {NI_CALLBACK_ID} 
	if(NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE{int} {NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE}  = NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE_LEFT_BUTTON_DOWN{int} {NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE_LEFT_BUTTON_DOWN} )
		transition_speed0{real} {transition_speed0}  := xy_center_circles[0]{real} {xy_center_circles}  - 0.5
		subarticulation_modulation_strength01{real} {subarticulation_modulation_strength01}  := sqrt((transition_speed0{real} {transition_speed0}  * transition_speed0{real} {transition_speed0} ) + (dy0{real} {dy0}  * dy0{real} {dy0} )){Builtin, None}
		distance0[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} {NI_CALLBACK_ID}  mod 100]{real} {distance0}  := subarticulation_modulation_strength01{real} {subarticulation_modulation_strength01} 
		subarticulation_modulation_strength01{real} {subarticulation_modulation_strength01}  := xy_center_circles[0]{real} {xy_center_circles}  - 0.5
		dy0{real} {dy0}  := xy_center_circles[1]{real} {xy_center_circles}  - 0.5
		cos_theta0{real} {cos_theta0}  := subarticulation_modulation_strength01{real} {subarticulation_modulation_strength01}  / sqrt((subarticulation_modulation_strength01{real} {subarticulation_modulation_strength01}  * subarticulation_modulation_strength01{real} {subarticulation_modulation_strength01} ) + (dy0{real} {dy0}  * dy0{real} {dy0} )){Builtin, None}
		angle1{real} {angle1}  := acos(cos_theta0{real} {cos_theta0} ){Builtin, None}
		if(dy0{real} {dy0}  < 0)
			angle1{real} {angle1}  := (2 * NI_MATH_PI{real} {NI_MATH_PI} ) - angle1{real} {angle1} 
		end if
		transition_speed0{real} {transition_speed0}  := angle1{real} {angle1} 
		angle2[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} {NI_CALLBACK_ID}  mod 100]{real} {angle2}  := transition_speed0{real} {transition_speed0} 
		dy0{real} {dy0}  := angle2[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} {NI_CALLBACK_ID}  mod 100]{real} {angle2} 
		subarticulation_modulation_strength01{real} {subarticulation_modulation_strength01}  := 0.7

function update_instrument_range
	iii1{int} {iii1}  := 128
	_ret6200{int} {_ret6200}  := 0
	group_count000{int} {group_count000}  := 0
	group_count001{int} {group_count001}  := 0
	while(group_count001{int} {group_count001}  <= 7) 
		if(_keyswitch_states[(ii4{int} {ii4}  * 8) + group_count001{int} {group_count001} ]{int} {_keyswitch_states}  = 1)
			group_count000{int} {group_count000}  := 0
			while(group_count000{int} {group_count000}  <= 3) 
				if(_loaded_subarticulations[(ii4{int} {ii4}  * 32) + ((group_count001{int} {group_count001}  * 4) + group_count000{int} {group_count000} )]{int} {_loaded_subarticulations}  >= 0)
					if(subarticulations_range_lower[subarticulations_ids_positions[_loaded_subarticulations[(ii4{int} {ii4}  * 32) + ((group_count001{int} {group_count001}  * 4) + group_count000{int} {group_count000} )]{int} {_loaded_subarticulations} ]{int} {subarticulations_ids_positions} ]{int} {subarticulations_range_lower}  < iii1{int} {iii1} )
						iii1{int} {iii1}  := subarticulations_range_lower[subarticulations_ids_positions[_loaded_subarticulations[(ii4{int} {ii4}  * 32) + ((group_count001{int} {group_count001}  * 4) + group_count000{int} {group_count000} )]{int} {_loaded_subarticulations} ]{int} {subarticulations_ids_positions} ]{int} {subarticulations_range_lower} 
					end if
					if(subarticulations_range_upper[subarticulations_ids_positions[_loaded_subarticulations[(ii4{int} {ii4}  * 32) + ((group_count001{int} {group_count001}  * 4) + group_count000{int} {group_count000} )]{int} {_loaded_subarticulations} ]{int} {subarticulations_ids_positions} ]{int} {subarticulations_range_upper}  > _ret6200{int} {_ret6200} )
						_ret6200{int} {_ret6200}  := subarticulations_range_upper[subarticulations_ids_positions[_loaded_subarticulations[(ii4{int} {ii4}  * 32) + ((group_count001{int} {group_count001}  * 4) + group_count000{int} {group_count000} )]{int} {_loaded_subarticulations} ]{int} {subarticulations_ids_positions} ]{int} {subarticulations_range_upper} 
					end if
				end if
				inc(group_count000{int} {group_count000} ){Builtin, None}
			end while
		end if
		inc(group_count001{int} {group_count001} ){Builtin, None}
	end while
	_instrument_range[ii4{int} {ii4}  * 2]{int} {_instrument_range}  := (iii1{int} {iii1}  - range_offset_lower{int} {range_offset_lower} ) - (octave_shift[ii4{int} {ii4} ]{int} {octave_shift}  * 12)
	_instrument_range[(ii4{int} {ii4}  * 2) + 1]{int} {_instrument_range}  := (_ret6200{int} {_ret6200}  + range_offset_upper{int} {range_offset_upper} ) - (octave_shift[ii4{int} {ii4} ]{int} {octave_shift}  * 12)
end function

	end while
end function

function keyswitches_on_note
	result13{int} {result13}  := 0
	dynamic_layer0{int} {dynamic_layer0}  := 0
	if(in_range(subarticulation_event1{int} {subarticulation_event1} , keyswitch_octave{int} {keyswitch_octave}  * 12, ((keyswitch_octave{int} {keyswitch_octave}  * 12) + 8) - 1){Builtin, None})
		i{int} {i}  := 0
		while(i{int} {i}  <= 7) 
			result13{int} {result13}  := _keyswitch_states[(selected_instrument{int} {selected_instrument}  * 8) + i{int} {i} ]{int} {_keyswitch_states} 
			_keyswitch_states[(selected_instrument{int} {selected_instrument}  * 8) + i{int} {i} ]{int} {_keyswitch_states}  := KEY_DOWN[(keyswitch_octave{int} {keyswitch_octave}  * 12) + i{int} {i} ]{int} {KEY_DOWN} 
			if(result13{int} {result13}  # _keyswitch_states[(selected_instrument{int} {selected_instrument}  * 8) + i{int} {i} ]{int} {_keyswitch_states} )
				dynamic_layer0{int} {dynamic_layer0}  := 1
			end if
			selected_keyswitch{int} {selected_keyswitch}  := subarticulation_event1{int} {subarticulation_event1}  - (keyswitch_octave{int} {keyswitch_octave}  * 12)
			inc(i{int} {i} ){Builtin, None}
		end while
		if(dynamic_layer0{int} {dynamic_layer0}  = 1)
			subarticulation_event1{int} {subarticulation_event1}  := end_note0{int} {end_note0} 
			call update_keyswitch_selection{UserDefined, Call}
		end if
	end if
end function

		wait(wait_time0[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} {NI_CALLBACK_ID}  mod 100]{int} {wait_time0} ){Builtin, None}
	end if
end function

function articulation_event_clear

	if(transition_type1{int} {transition_type1}  # -1)
		note3{int} {note3}  := 0
		while(note3{int} {note3}  <= 3) 
			_articulation_event_list[(transition_type1{int} {transition_type1}  * 4) + note3{int} {note3} ]{int} {_articulation_event_list}  := -1
			inc(note3{int} {note3} ){Builtin, None}
		end while
		articulation_event_instrument[transition_type1{int} {transition_type1} ]{int} {articulation_event_instrument}  := -1

function subarticulation_event_get_free_index

		if((subarticulation_event_list[group_count000{int} {group_count000} ]{int} {subarticulation_event_list}  = -1) and (subarticulation_event_last_used[group_count000{int} {group_count000} ]{int} {subarticulation_event_last_used}  < (ENGINE_UPTIME{int} {ENGINE_UPTIME}  - lookahead{int} {lookahead} )))
			group_count001{int} {group_count001}  := group_count000{int} {group_count000} 
			group_count000{int} {group_count000}  := 128
		end if
		group_count000{int} {group_count000}  := group_count000{int} {group_count000}  + 1
	end while
	lowest00{int} {lowest00}  := group_count001{int} {group_count001} 
end function

function last_transitions_update
	i12{int} {i12}  := 0
	while(i12{int} {i12}  <= (num_elements(_last_transitions{int[]} {_last_transitions} ){Builtin, None} - 1))

	else

end function

function find_loaded_legato
	authoring_page_active{int} {authoring_page_active}  := 0
	if(_loaded_subarticulations[0]{int} {_loaded_subarticulations}  # -1)
		if(subarticulations_type[subarticulations_ids_positions[_loaded_subarticulations[0]{int} {_loaded_subarticulations} ]{int} {subarticulations_ids_positions} ]{int} {subarticulations_type}  = 2)
			authoring_page_active{int} {authoring_page_active}  := 1
			set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(lbl_authoring_legato_title{int} {lbl_authoring_legato_title} ){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_TEXT{int} {CONTROL_PAR_TEXT} , subarticulations_full_name[subarticulations_ids_positions[_loaded_subarticulations[0]{int} {_loaded_subarticulations} ]{int} {subarticulations_ids_positions} ]{string} {subarticulations_full_name}  & " (" & _loaded_subarticulations[0]{int} {_loaded_subarticulations}  & ")"){Builtin, None}
		end if
	end if
end function

function authoring_open
	call find_loaded_legato{UserDefined, Call}
	start_note0{int} {start_note0}  := 60
	end_note0{int} {end_note0}  := 60
	dynamic_layer0{int} {dynamic_layer0}  := 0
	call update_authoring_transition{UserDefined, Call}
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(pnl_authoring{int} {pnl_authoring} ){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int} {CONTROL_PAR_HIDE} , HIDE_PART_NOTHING{int} {HIDE_PART_NOTHING} ){Builtin, None}
end function

function update_subarticulation_selection
	group_count001{int} {group_count001}  := selected_subarticulation{int} {selected_subarticulation} 
	group_count000{int} {group_count000}  := 0
	while(group_count000{int} {group_count000}  <= (num_elements(btn_edit_subarticulation_selection{int[]} {btn_edit_subarticulation_selection} ){Builtin, None} - 1)) 
		if(group_count000{int} {group_count000}  # group_count001{int} {group_count001} )
			set_control_par(btn_edit_subarticulation_selection[group_count000{int} {group_count000} ]{int} {btn_edit_subarticulation_selection} , CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int} {CONTROL_PAR_VALUE} , 0){Builtin, None}
		else
			set_control_par(btn_edit_subarticulation_selection[group_count000{int} {group_count000} ]{int} {btn_edit_subarticulation_selection} , CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int} {CONTROL_PAR_VALUE} , 1){Builtin, None}
		end if
		inc(group_count000{int} {group_count000} ){Builtin, None}
	end while
	if(_loaded_subarticulations[(selected_instrument{int} {selected_instrument}  * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} {selected_keyswitch}  * 4) + selected_subarticulation{int} {selected_subarticulation} )]{int} {_loaded_subarticulations}  # -1)
		set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(btn_subarticulation_title{int} {btn_subarticulation_title} ){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_TEXT{int} {CONTROL_PAR_TEXT} , "    " & subarticulations_full_name[subarticulations_ids_positions[_loaded_subarticulations[(selected_instrument{int} {selected_instrument}  * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} {selected_keyswitch}  * 4) + selected_subarticulation{int} {selected_subarticulation} )]{int} {_loaded_subarticulations} ]{int} {subarticulations_ids_positions} ]{string} {subarticulations_full_name} ){Builtin, None}
	else
		set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(btn_subarticulation_title{int} {btn_subarticulation_title} ){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_TEXT{int} {CONTROL_PAR_TEXT} , "    Empty"){Builtin, None}

function subarticulation_browser_open
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(pnl_subarticulation_browser{int} {pnl_subarticulation_browser} ){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int} {CONTROL_PAR_HIDE} , HIDE_PART_NOTHING{int} {HIDE_PART_NOTHING} ){Builtin, None}
	if(_loaded_subarticulations[(selected_instrument{int} {selected_instrument}  * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} {selected_keyswitch}  * 4) + selected_subarticulation{int} {selected_subarticulation} )]{int} {_loaded_subarticulations}  # -1)
		idx25{int} {idx25}  := type_to_category[subarticulations_type[subarticulations_ids_positions[_loaded_subarticulations[(selected_instrument{int} {selected_instrument}  * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} {selected_keyswitch}  * 4) + selected_subarticulation{int} {selected_subarticulation} )]{int} {_loaded_subarticulations} ]{int} {subarticulations_ids_positions} ]{int} {subarticulations_type} ]{int} {type_to_category} 
		subarticulation_event1{int} {subarticulation_event1}  := 0
		while(subarticulation_event1{int} {subarticulation_event1}  <= (num_elements(btn_subarticulation_browser_selection{int[]} {btn_subarticulation_browser_selection} ){Builtin, None} - 1)) 
			set_control_par(btn_subarticulation_browser_selection[subarticulation_event1{int} {subarticulation_event1} ]{int} {btn_subarticulation_browser_selection} , CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int} {CONTROL_PAR_HIDE} , HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL{int} {HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL} ){Builtin, None}
			if(_subarticulation_browser_entries[(selected_instrument{int} {selected_instrument}  * 98) + ((idx25{int} {idx25}  * 14) + subarticulation_event1{int} {subarticulation_event1} )]{int} {_subarticulation_browser_entries}  # -1)
				set_control_par_str(btn_subarticulation_browser_selection[subarticulation_event1{int} {subarticulation_event1} ]{int} {btn_subarticulation_browser_selection} , CONTROL_PAR_TEXT{int} {CONTROL_PAR_TEXT} , subarticulations_full_name[subarticulations_ids_positions[_subarticulation_browser_entries[(selected_instrument{int} {selected_instrument}  * 98) + ((idx25{int} {idx25}  * 14) + subarticulation_event1{int} {subarticulation_event1} )]{int} {_subarticulation_browser_entries} ]{int} {subarticulations_ids_positions} ]{string} {subarticulations_full_name} ){Builtin, None}
				if(_subarticulation_browser_entries[(selected_instrument{int} {selected_instrument}  * 98) + ((idx25{int} {idx25}  * 14) + subarticulation_event1{int} {subarticulation_event1} )]{int} {_subarticulation_browser_entries}  = _loaded_subarticulations[(selected_instrument{int} {selected_instrument}  * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} {selected_keyswitch}  * 4) + selected_subarticulation{int} {selected_subarticulation} )]{int} {_loaded_subarticulations} )
					set_control_par(btn_subarticulation_browser_selection[subarticulation_event1{int} {subarticulation_event1} ]{int} {btn_subarticulation_browser_selection} , CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int} {CONTROL_PAR_VALUE} , 1){Builtin, None}
				else
					set_control_par(btn_subarticulation_browser_selection[subarticulation_event1{int} {subarticulation_event1} ]{int} {btn_subarticulation_browser_selection} , CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int} {CONTROL_PAR_VALUE} , 0){Builtin, None}
				end if
				set_control_par(btn_subarticulation_browser_selection[subarticulation_event1{int} {subarticulation_event1} ]{int} {btn_subarticulation_browser_selection} , CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int} {CONTROL_PAR_HIDE} , HIDE_PART_NOTHING{int} {HIDE_PART_NOTHING} ){Builtin, None}
			end if
			inc(subarticulation_event1{int} {subarticulation_event1} ){Builtin, None}
		end while
		subarticulation_event1{int} {subarticulation_event1}  := 0
		while(subarticulation_event1{int} {subarticulation_event1}  <= (num_elements(btn_subarticulation_browser_category{int[]} {btn_subarticulation_browser_category} ){Builtin, None} - 1)) 
			if(subarticulation_event1{int} {subarticulation_event1}  = idx25{int} {idx25} )

		end while

function angle_to_value
	angle1{real} {angle1}  := dy0{real} {dy0}  + (NI_MATH_PI{real} {NI_MATH_PI}  / 2)
	if(angle1{real} {angle1}  > (NI_MATH_PI{real} {NI_MATH_PI}  * 2))
		angle1{real} {angle1}  := angle1{real} {angle1}  - (2 * NI_MATH_PI{real} {NI_MATH_PI} )
	end if
	angle1{real} {angle1}  := abs(angle1{real} {angle1}  - (2 * NI_MATH_PI{real} {NI_MATH_PI} )){Builtin, None}
	result13{int} {result13}  := int((127 * (angle1{real} {angle1}  - subarticulation_modulation_strength01{real} {subarticulation_modulation_strength01} )) / (transition_speed0{real} {transition_speed0}  - subarticulation_modulation_strength01{real} {subarticulation_modulation_strength01} )){Builtin, None}
end function
